SPR_the_inevitable_civil_war = {

	SPA_military_plot_nationalists = {

		priority = 10

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 250

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		is_good = yes

		timeout_effect = {
			country_event = lar_spain.2
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = SPA_awaiting_the_rebellion
				}
				remove_ideas = SPA_awaiting_the_rebellion
			}
		}
	}

	SPR_military_plot_republicans = {

		priority = 10

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		days_mission_timeout = 250

		fire_only_once = yes

		activation = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		is_good = no

		timeout_effect = {
			country_event = lar_spain.2
		}
	}

	SPA_primo_de_rivera_speech = {

		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPA_primo_de_rivera_imprisoned
				has_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
			}
		}

		cost = 30

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}

		days_remove = 37

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
			    ideology = fascism
			    popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPA_military_plot_nationalists
				days = -36
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_primo_de_rivera_first_speech }
				}
				set_country_flag = SPR_primo_de_rivera_first_speech
			}
		}

	}

	SPA_sway_leader_loyalty = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
			}
		}

		cost = 30

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}

		days_remove = 37

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPA_military_plot_nationalists
				days = -36
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies }
					NOT = { has_id = 1108 }
					NOT = { has_character_flag = SPR_do_not_align_me_flag }
				}
				add_unit_leader_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies
				set_unit_leader_flag = SPA_swayed_leader_loyalty_flag
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

	}

	SPR_secure_leader_loyalty = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {

				has_unit_leader_flag = SPA_swayed_leader_loyalty_flag

				mission = SPR_military_plot_republicans
				days = 37
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies

				}
				remove_unit_leader_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies
				clr_unit_leader_flag = SPA_swayed_leader_loyalty_flag
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

	}

		remove_effect = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {

				days = 37

					has_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies

						has_unit_leader_flag = SPR_reassigned_flag
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_reassign_disloyal_leader_tt
				set_unit_leader_flag = SPR_reassigned_flag # Generates trait upon SCW start that makes them useless for 60 days.
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

	}

	SPA_expand_influence_in_the_galicia_garrison = {

		icon = {
			key = spa_garrison_control_none
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				830 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spa_garrison_control_weak
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				830 = {
					check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = equals }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = SPA_northern_garrisons_state_flag }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spa_garrison_control_weak2
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				830 = {
					check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = equals }

			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spr_garrison_control_none
			trigger = {

		}

		icon = {

				has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				830 = {

		}
		icon = {
			key = spr_garrison_control_total
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				830 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			}
		}

		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 830
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_trigger_tt
					830 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_trigger_tt
					830 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
 highlight_state_targets = { state = 830 state = 833 state = 887 state = 874 state = 2779 } 
}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 830.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 14

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_galicia_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
				
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_galicia_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				830 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_secure_the_northern_garrisons }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				830 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				830 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spa_garrison_control_strong
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 3 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spa_garrison_control_total
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spr_garrison_control_none
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spr_garrison_control_weak
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spr_garrison_control_strong
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 3 compare = equals } }
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = spr_garrison_control_total
			trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 4 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
			}
		}

		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 837
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_trigger_tt
					837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_trigger_tt
					837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
 highlight_state_targets = { state = 837 } 
}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 837.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 14

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_asturias_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_asturias_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				837 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				837 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

		highlight_states = {
 highlight_state_targets = { state = 859 } 
}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 859.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 14

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_burgos_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_burgos_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				859 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_secure_the_northern_garrisons }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				859 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				859 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 10
			}
		}
	}

				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_west_aragon_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}

						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

			base = 110
			modifier = {
				880 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain

		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 951
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_trigger_tt
					951 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			if = {

				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
 highlight_state_targets = { state = 951 } 
}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 951.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 14

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_madrid_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_madrid_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				951 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				factor = 100
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

			}
		}

		available = {
			has_full_control_of_state = 1029
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_trigger_tt
					1029 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 4 compare = less_than } }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_trigger_tt
					1029 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
 highlight_state_targets = { state = 1029 } 
}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 1029.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 14

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_ciudad_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_ciudad_group = yes
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				1029 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				1029 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				1029 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}

						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				1058 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				1058 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5

			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_military_plot_republicans
				days = -25
			}
			add_popularity = {
			    ideology = fascism
			    popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -15
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SPR_primo_de_rivera_first_speech }
				}
				set_country_flag = SPR_primo_de_rivera_first_speech
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = lar_spain.4 }
			}
		}

	}

					NOT = { has_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies }

					NOT = { has_character_flag = SPR_do_not_align_me_flag }
				}

	SPA_expand_influence_in_the_galicia_garrison_mission = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
 highlight_state_targets = { state = 830 } 
}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 14

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_galicia_group = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
						date < 1936.5.2
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 45 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
						date > 1936.5.1
						date < 1936.8.10
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 30 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
						date > 1936.8.9
						date < 1936.10.2
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 21 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
						date > 1936.10.1
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front }
						date < 1936.7.20
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front }
						date > 1936.7.19
						date < 1936.9.16
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 30 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front }
						date > 1936.9.15
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 45 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_galicia_group = yes
				}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_galicia_group = yes
				}
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
						SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.7.20
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.7.19
							date < 1936.9.16
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 5 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.9.15
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 15 random_days = 15 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_galicia_group = yes
				}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_galicia_group = yes
				}
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.5.2
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 20 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.5.1
							date < 1936.8.10
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 6 random_days = 9 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.8.9
							date < 1936.10.2
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 1 random_days = 5 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.10.1
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 45 }
				}
			}

				}

					}

						}

					}
					if = {
						limit = {

							date < 1936.9.16

					}
					if = {
						limit = {

						}

					}
				}

				limit = {
					is_navarra_group = yes
				}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_navarra_group = yes
				}
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
						SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.7.20
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.7.19
							date < 1936.9.16
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 5 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.9.15
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 15 random_days = 15 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_navarra_group = yes
				}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_navarra_group = yes
				}
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.5.2
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 20 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.5.1
							date < 1936.8.10
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 6 random_days = 9 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.8.9
							date < 1936.10.2
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 1 random_days = 5 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.10.1
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}

					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_salamanca_group = yes
				}
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
						SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.7.20
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.7.19
							date < 1936.9.16
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 5 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.9.15
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 15 random_days = 15 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_salamanca_group = yes
				}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_salamanca_group = yes
				}
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.5.2
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 20 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.5.1
							date < 1936.8.10
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 6 random_days = 9 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.8.9
							date < 1936.10.2

				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_extremadura_group = yes
				}
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
						SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.7.20
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.7.19
							date < 1936.9.16
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 5 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.9.15
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 15 random_days = 15 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_extremadura_group = yes
				}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_extremadura_group = yes
				}
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.5.2
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 20 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.5.1
							date < 1936.8.10
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 6 random_days = 9 }
					}
					if = {

		}

		visible = {

					}

						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
						SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.7.20
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.7.19
							date < 1936.9.16
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 5 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.9.15
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 15 random_days = 15 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_cordoba_group = yes
				}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_cordoba_group = yes
				}
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date < 1936.5.2
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 20 random_days = 10 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.5.1
							date < 1936.8.10
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 6 random_days = 9 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.8.9
							date < 1936.10.2
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 1 random_days = 5 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.10.1
						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 }
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

	SPA_expand_influence_in_the_granada_garrison_mission = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
 highlight_state_targets = { state = 1083 } 
}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 14

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_granada_group = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
						date < 1936.5.2
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 45 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
						date > 1936.5.1
						date < 1936.8.10
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 30 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
						date > 1936.8.9
						date < 1936.10.2
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 21 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
						date > 1936.10.1
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front }
						date < 1936.7.20
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front }
						date > 1936.7.19
						date < 1936.9.16
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 30 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front }
						date > 1936.9.15
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 45 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_granada_group = yes
				}
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					every_state = {

						if = {

							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }

						SPR_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
					}
					if = {

							date < 1936.7.20
						}

					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							date > 1936.7.19
							date < 1936.9.16
						}

					}

						}
						country_event = { id = lar_spain.5 days = 15 random_days = 15 }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {

				}

SPR_civil_war_offensives = {

	SPA_galicia_offensive = {

		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 830 }
			NOT = { has_active_mission = SPR_preparing_offensive }
			830 = {
				has_state_flag = SPR_unplanned_offensive_flag
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { state = 830 } 
 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 14

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = SPR
			has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
			NOT = { has_global_flag = scw_over }
			830 = { has_state_flag = SPR_unplanned_offensive_flag }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			activate_mission = SPR_preparing_offensive
			set_country_flag = SPR_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SPR
				}
				activate_mission = SPA_galicia_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_galicia_group = yes
				}
				clr_state_flag = SPR_unplanned_offensive_flag
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = unplanned_offensive
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
					830 = { is_controlled_by = SPD }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_republican_offensive days = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
						has_completed_focus = SPR_take_the_initiative
					}
					830 = { is_controlled_by = SPC }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_anarchist_offensive days = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
						has_completed_focus = SPR_take_the_initiative
					}
					830 = { is_controlled_by = SPB }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_carlist_offensive days = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_take_the_initiative
					830 = { is_controlled_by = SPA }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPR_anti_nationalist_offensive days = 30 }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_full_control_of_state = 830
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					tag = SPA
					tag = SPB
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				divisions_in_state = {
					state = 830
					size > 0
				}
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 830
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SPR
				}
				activate_mission = SPA_salamanca_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_salamanca_group = yes
				}
				clr_state_flag = SPR_unplanned_offensive_flag
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = unplanned_offensive
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
					943 = { is_controlled_by = SPR }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_republican_offensive days = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
					943 = { is_controlled_by = SPC }
				}

				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_carlist_offensive days = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_take_the_initiative
					943 = { is_controlled_by = SPA }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPR_anti_nationalist_offensive days = 30 }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_full_control_of_state = 943
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					tag = SPA
					tag = SPB
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				divisions_in_state = {
					state = 943
					size > 0
				}
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 943
				}
			}
		}

 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 14

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = SPR
			has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
			NOT = { has_global_flag = scw_over }
			1079 = { has_state_flag = SPR_unplanned_offensive_flag }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			activate_mission = SPR_preparing_offensive
			set_country_flag = SPR_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = SPR
				}
				activate_mission = SPA_sevilla_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_sevilla_group = yes
				}
				clr_state_flag = SPR_unplanned_offensive_flag
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = unplanned_offensive
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
					1079 = { is_controlled_by = SPR }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_republican_offensive days = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
					1079 = { is_controlled_by = SPC }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_anarchist_offensive days = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_tackle_the_vulnerable_fronts
					1079 = { is_controlled_by = SPB }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPA_anti_carlist_offensive days = 30 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_take_the_initiative
					1079 = { is_controlled_by = SPA }
				}
				add_timed_idea = { idea = SPR_anti_nationalist_offensive days = 30 }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_full_control_of_state = 1079
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					tag = SPA
					tag = SPB
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				divisions_in_state = {
					state = 1079
					size > 0
				}
				NOT = {
					has_full_control_of_state = 1079
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

		}

		}
	}

			original_tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
	 		highlight_state_targets = { state = 951 } 
	 		highlight_color_while_active = 1
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_mission_timeout = 14

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			original_tag = SPR
			has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
			NOT = { has_global_flag = scw_over }
			951 = { has_state_flag = SPR_unplanned_offensive_flag }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_madrid_group = yes
				}
				clr_state_flag = SPR_unplanned_offensive_flag
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = unplanned_offensive
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SPA_activate_galicia_fifth_columnists = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		allowed = {
			tag = SPA
		}

		available = {
			830 = {
				NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT }
				any_neighbor_state = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
 highlight_state_targets = { state = 830 } 
}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 25

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 30

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPA
			has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
			NOT = { has_global_flag = scw_over }
			830 = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } }
			has_completed_focus = SPA_the_fifth_column
		}

		complete_effect = {
			
		}

		remove_effect = {
			830 = {
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Fifth Columnist Brigade\"	start_experience_factor = 0	start_equipment_factor = 1"
					owner = ROOT
					allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					count = 2
					country_score = {
						base = 100
						modifier = {
							tag = SPR
							add = 100
						}
						modifier = {
							tag = SPB
							add = 100
						}
						modifier = {
							tag = SPC
							add = 100
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

political_actions = {
	
	SPA_carlist_uprising_mission = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		allowed = {
			tag = SPA
		}

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_the_phalanx_ascendant
				}
				hidden_trigger = { always = no }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_unify_the_nationalist_front
				}
				has_completed_focus = SPA_fuse_the_parties
			}
		}

		priority = 10

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_mission_timeout = 316

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_the_phalanx_ascendant
				}
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_eliminate_the_carlists }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_unify_the_nationalist_front
				}
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_fuse_the_parties }
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_controlled_states > 4
				}
				country_event = lar_spain.7
			}
			else = {
				activate_mission = SPA_carlist_uprising_mission
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = SPA_carlist_uprising_mission
					days = -316
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SPR_anarchist_uprising_mission = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

			tag = SPR

		name = SPA_save_the_alcazar

		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns

		allowed = {
			tag = SPA
		}

		available = {
			controls_province = 858
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_mission_timeout = 140

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
			has_completed_focus = SPA_save_the_alcazar
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_war_support = 0.1
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_political_power = 100
			complete_national_focus = SPA_caudillo_of_spain
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPA_carlist_uprising_mission
				days = 70
			}
		}

		timeout_effect = {
		}
	}

}

SPA_reassert_american_dominance = {
	
	SPA_reassert_dominance = {

		icon = eng_trade_unions_demand

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			strength_ratio = {
			    tag = FROM
			    ratio > 2
			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						is_on_continent = south_america
						is_on_continent = north_america
					}
				}
				NOT = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = {
					original_tag = HOL
					original_tag = DEN
					original_tag = FRA
					original_tag = ENG
					original_tag = CAN
					original_tag = USA
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = SPA_reassert_american_dominance
			tag = SPA
		}

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = { country_event = lar_spain.19 }
		}
	}

SPR_the_seeds_of_revolution = {

	SPR_integrate_commune_1 = {

		name = SPR_integrate_commune

		icon = generic_nationalism

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			FROM = {
				compliance > 50
				OR = {
					is_island_state = yes
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		state_target = yes

		on_map_mode = map_only

		#targets = {  }

		target_array = controlled_states

		target_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_global_defense_council
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
				OR = {
					is_island_state = yes
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_core_of = ROOT
					}
				}
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
					}
					is_mainland_spain_vanilla_groups = no
				}
				compliance > 35
			}
		}

		cost = 50

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 60

		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -1
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPC
			has_completed_focus = SPR_global_defense_council
			always = yes
		}

		complete_effect = {

		}

		remove_effect = {
			FROM = {
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			transfer_state = FROM
		}
	}

	SPR_integrate_commune_2 = {

	SPR_ignite_uprising = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		allowed = {
			original_tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			FROM = {
				has_civil_war = no
				any_controlled_state = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					is_capital = no
				}
			}
			has_equipment = {
			    infantry_equipment > 19999
			}
			any_controlled_state = {
				NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
			}
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
				any_controlled_state = {
					is_in_home_area = yes
					any_neighbor_state = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 150

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = 90

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPC
			has_completed_focus = SPR_plant_the_seeds_of_revolution
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			    type = infantry_equipment
			    amount = -20000
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					set_country_flag = SPR_ignite_uprising_timer_flag
					activate_mission = SPR_ignite_uprising_timer_mission
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						any_controlled_state = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							is_capital = no
							NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
							any_state = {
								is_controlled_by = ROOT
								NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
								distance_to = {
									target = PREV
									value < 750
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = FROM
						is_in_home_area = yes
						is_capital = no
						NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
						any_state = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
							distance_to = {
								target = PREV
								value < 750
							}
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = anarchist_uprising
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
						owner = ROOT
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
						owner = ROOT
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
						owner = ROOT
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						any_controlled_state = {
							is_in_home_area = yes
							is_capital = no
							NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
							any_state = {
								is_controlled_by = ROOT
								NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
								distance_to = {
									target = PREV
									value < 1500
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = FROM
						is_in_home_area = yes
						is_capital = no
						NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
						any_state = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
							distance_to = {
								target = PREV
								value < 1500
							}
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = anarchist_uprising
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
						owner = ROOT
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
						owner = ROOT
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
						owner = ROOT
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_state = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = FROM
						is_in_home_area = yes
						is_capital = no
						NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
						any_state = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							NOT = { has_state_flag = anarchist_uprising }
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = anarchist_uprising
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
						owner = ROOT
						allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
						owner = ROOT

							division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
							owner = ROOT
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
						create_unit = {
							division = "division_template = \"Anarchist Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1" 
							owner = ROOT
							allow_spawning_on_enemy_provs = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

	}

		}

				has_completed_focus = SPA_stamp_out_the_maquis
				has_completed_focus = SPR_the_inevitable_counterblow
				has_completed_focus = SPR_all_must_do_their_part
				has_completed_focus = SPR_red_bulwark_in_the_west
				has_completed_focus = SPR_stabilize_the_nation
			}
